“If sentient beings indulge the three karmic actions and six senses, commit the ten evils, the five rebellious acts, and boundless transgressions, then upon death they will enter the nine dark hells of Fengdu, where each offense is examined and punished. They shall endure bitter agonies for ten thousand kalpas before rebirth. This is what is meant by not nonexistent.”

Since it is known to be not nonexistent, one must seek repentance. A single day of self-reflection, awakening, and repentance dissolves the sins of ten thousand kalpas. How is the power of this repentance known? In ancient times, there was a man born foolish and ignorant, who committed myriad sins. One day, he reflected and awakened; witnessing the five signs of decay, he was seized with terror and took refuge in the Three Treasures. Thereupon, the roots of his decay and transgressions instantly dissolved, and his heavenly years were prolonged. Thus, all here present, with the teachings clearly expounded, know that repentance enables sentient beings to avoid hell and its manifold sufferings.

If one does not encounter a good spiritual guide, evil karma deepens. They may know only to wash away the grease and grime from the body but fail to sweep the dust from the heart. Thus, at life’s end, they enter hell and endure the weight of their transgressions. At such a time, remorse and fear come too late. Body and mind are shattered, spirit and soul scattered. The wind-knives stand before them; repentance is no longer possible. What recourse remains for their suffering?

All you sentient beings, do not rely on your prime of life, do not cling to wealth and treasure, do not become attached to family and kin. Do not indulge in fleeting pleasures, courting the agony of death. When the great limit arrives, it spares neither rich nor poor, neither old nor young, neither noble nor base—all are ground to nothingness. Like the wind’s lamp or spark from stone, what endures? Like lightning at noon or morning dew, what is firm?

When the five celestial messengers and the death-dealing ghosts of impermanence arrive, even youth and radiant beauty cannot resist. At that moment, grand halls and secluded chambers become irrelevant; fine carriages and mighty steeds cannot follow; wives, children, and kin are no longer one’s own; the seven treasures and precious ornaments become playthings for others. The Merciful Honored One said: In the Red Clarity Kalpa of old, there was a sentient being, sharp-witted and intelligent, who subdued afflictions. Though wealthy, he refused to give alms to the poor. When his life ended, he fell into the animal realm, reborn as a red fox, enduring karmic retribution in full. All you sentient beings, be ever vigilant—lest in a single morning you be bound to such suffering, when regret comes too late.

Consider this: in the world of the living, if one faces even a minor matter and must enter the public court, though the offense be slight, the heart trembles in fear. Kinfolk grow anxious, exhausting every means to seek deliverance. How much more so for the beings in hell? Compared to them, such distress is but a shadow.

Countless hells, numbering in the hundreds of thousands, are all governed within this celestial realm. Located in the far north, beyond the Northern Heavens, past boundless, measureless dark abysses, there lies a world called the Five Qi Mystic Heaven, the Dark North, the Solitary, Profound, and Utmost Land. Within it, the Five Qi Five Spirits Mystic Elder Black Emperor Heavenly Lord presides over the northern quarter, restraining the yin demons.

Beneath this land lies the Great Void, the Vast Wilderness, and the boundless, fathomless Black Sea. Its waters are vile, its shores unknowable. At its center rises a great mountain, piercing the azure heavens above and plunging into the windy springs below—Mount Fengdu of the North. It towers one million six hundred thousand *li* high, with a circumference of five hundred thousand *li*. Its base sinks fifteen thousand *li* into the water. At the water’s edge, where the mountain’s foot meets the sea, lies a vast cavern called the Yin Shadow Heaven, the land known as Great Yin.

Beneath the Water Emperor are thirty-six lesser hells, each walled in iron, ninefold encircled. Within each hell, grasses and trees arise from the naturally venomous qi, their branches and leaves transformed into blades and swords, their edges sharp and plentiful. Fierce beasts, scorching smoke, and black winds rage ceaselessly, day and night. The darkness is profound, poisonous qi and bloody light surge, and the stench of filth and decay fills the air. The light of sun, moon, and stars cannot penetrate these hells.

Thirty-seven kings preside, each over one hell. Within each, seventy tiers of knife-forests stand, along with countless iron nets. Fire blazes from above, flames surge from below, intertwining like fish in a searing pan. The iron-walled cities have four gates, and at each gate stand four great bronze dogs, each body spanning forty *li*. When they roar, the iron walls tremble. Their fangs are like forests of swords, their claws sharp and forms ferocious—beyond compare.

There are also countless iron birds, each over a *zhang* in size, with beaks of bronze and claws of iron. They beat their wings in flight, eyes like shooting stars, feathers like iron arrows, each tipped with swirling flames. When they shriek, their cries shake the earth like thunderbolts. Fire spews from their beaks and feathers, and all such creatures devour the marrow of the damned. The pain of the condemned is beyond description, their suffering piercing to the liver and heart. For immeasurable ages, they seek life but find none, seek respite but receive none.

Today, in this ritual assembly, as the sutras describe, such hells exist—boundless and unceasing, their torments endless. Through this rite of repentance, we extend our prayers to all hells, that those enduring suffering may attain liberation.

The repentant one, [Name], prostrates for peace and offers this repentance text, bowing with utmost reverence, listening with single-minded devotion. With bowed head, we pay homage to the Merciful Honored One and reverently venerate the true sages:

With sincere heart, we bow to the Jade Clarity Bestower of Blessings Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Saves Upon Hearing the Cry.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Transcendent Immortals.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Supreme Perfected Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Wondrously Serene Golden Light Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Fulfilled Merit and Virtue.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ever-Shining Dharma Lamp.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Ferries Across on the Jeweled Boat.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ever-Pure Dharma Sea.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Commands the Registrar of Life.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Boundless Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Delivers from Ten Sufferings.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Protects the Realm.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Manifest Responses.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Jeweled King.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Supreme One Who Saves from Suffering.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Grants Longevity.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion and Realm-Protection.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Bliss.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Aspiration.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Unified Dao.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit and Virtue.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Perfected of Azure Mystery.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Three Heavens’ Perfected.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Greatly Compassionate Perfected Who Saves from Suffering.
With sincere heart, we bow to the Greatly Merciful Perfected Who Delivers from Sin.

Today, the repentant one and this great assembly humbly pray to the Supreme Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Northeast, to all the honored ones, all the sages, all the great perfected, all the great transformers, all the great immortals, and all the youthful saviors of suffering, who pervade the ten directions, fill the boundless void, and respond to every invocation of the true and sacred.

May the subtle and wondrous radiance of their hair-tips illuminate the hells of Mount Fengdu. For the repentant one, [Name], and those of the past—nine generations of ancestors, seven lineages of kin, parents of three lifetimes, uncles, brothers, and all family—who may be confined in darkness, enduring torment, may they swiftly attain liberation through the power of this repentance, the power of merit and virtue, and the inconceivable power, ascending to the Dao of non-action.

A Bow: Expounding the Thirty-Seven Hells, Second Scroll

Today, the assembly of this Daoist sanctuary, each with concentrated mind, reverently faces the Merciful Honored One to recite the names of the thirty-seven hells.

The repentant one, [Name], gathers his thoughts, kneels in reverence, and listens attentively to the exposition:

In Fengdu’s Mount Luoshan, to the east, west, south, and north, thirty-six hells are arrayed. At their center lies one hell, called the Northern Mount Luoshan, the Great Avīci Hell of Uninterrupted Suffering.

The Universal Savior speaks: “To the east, west, south, and north, thirty-six hells in all—may we hear their names.”

The Merciful Honored One replies:
To the east are nine hells: Heavenly One, Heavenly Overseer, Heavenly Leveler, Heavenly Void, Heavenly Sovereign, Nine Heavens, Primordial Rectitude, Punitive Rectitude, and Great Perfected.
To the south are nine hells: Flowing Fire, Fire Pellets, Fire Arrows, Flying Fire, Burning Feet, Fire Elephant, Burning Body, Primordial Leveler, and Prohibitive Punishment.
To the west are nine hells: Iron Chariots, Iron Horses, Iron Oxen, Iron Donkeys, Iron Awls, Iron Beds, Iron Staffs, Iron Chains, and Iron Rakes.
To the north are nine hells: Dark Sands, Northern Darkness, Female Azure, River Earl, Profound Darkness, Accumulated Kalpas, Statutory Decrees, Excrement and Urine, and Ice Pools.

These thirty-six hells, each governed by the karmic deeds of beings, administer punishment according to their offenses.

At their center lies one hell, where those guilty of the ten evils and five heinous crimes are confined. Within it stand:
Knife Mountains and Sword Trees,
Cauldrons of Boiling Water and Furnaces of Burning Coals,
Molten Copper Pillars,
Iron Plows and Iron Pellets,
Iron Awls and Iron Mills,
Iron Pestles and Iron Mountains,
Iron Nails and Iron Cangues,
Iron Rods and Iron Scales,
Iron Shackles and Iron Manacles,
Iron Locks and Iron Caskets,
Iron Birds and Ash Rivers,
Snow Mountains and Ice Wells,
Fire Pits and Dismemberment,
Strangulation and Sawing,
Flaying of Skin,
Stinking Turtles and Smoldering Embers,
Burning from Feet to Hands,
Blades, Needles, and Narrow Rocks,
Fire Mountains and Fire Mills—
countless torments, beyond numbering.

Within hangs a mirror that reflects the sins of the damned, revealing every hidden transgression. A moment there is like an eon passed. Ten thousand deaths and ten thousand rebirths, each agony more bitter than the last. No other hell compares.

The warden of this hell oversees all others, hence it is called the Great Central Hell.
*Avīci* means “great,” and *bi* means “to obstruct.” *Wu jian* means “without respite.” Thus, it is called the Great Avīci Hell of Uninterrupted Suffering.
Alternatively, *a* means “unceasing,” and *bi* means “unrelenting.” Torment and pain know no pause, no rest. Within, karmic winds blow upon the bodies and minds of the damned, shattering them into ten thousand deaths, only to revive them in an instant. Thus, in a single moment, ten thousand deaths and ten thousand rebirths occur—so it is in all the hells.

Here, the Great Emperor of Fengdu commands two hundred forty bureaus, overseeing fifty thousand minions who interrogate the damned, probing the weight of their sins, leaving no detail unexamined, and reporting all deeds, good and evil.

Consider the Iron Chariot, engulfed in fierce flames, ever ablaze. A yakṣa dwells within; from afar, the damned see it as a fair maiden and long to approach. Yet upon entering, their flesh and bones turn to ash and smoke.

The Iron Ox’s body, head, fur, horns, and tail are sharp as blades. From afar, the damned see it as a golden lotus, but upon reaching it, flames and smoke consume their bodies, leaving no trace.

The Iron Horse’s form, mane, and tail are keen as sword edges. The Iron Donkey is the same. Each is led by a yakṣa to the damned. When they mount, their bodies dissolve. The Iron Rakes and other implements of torment—cruel, vicious, and venomous, with raging fires and razor edges—are beyond description.

You, all beings, may hear of these torments but must never witness them. Should you encounter such a place, escape would be impossible for ten thousand kalpas.

Do not speak idly of hells and heavens. The unseen and the seen are equal; life and death are the same. It is like a man’s dream and his waking: death is as the dream, and birth as waking. What is done in dreams differs not from waking; what is done in death differs not from life. Joy in dreams is self-made; suffering in waking is self-caused.

You, all beings, should reflect deeply and seek early deliverance. The means to deliverance is none other than repentance. After repentance, abandon past wrongs and cultivate anew.

Moreover, in the Middle Kingdom, it is rare to obtain a human body. Rarer still is one who cultivates good fruits. Like the sun and moon, whose light shines impartially, illuminating all, leaving no darkness unlit—you, all beings, are neither blind nor deaf. The blind see not the sun and moon; the deaf hear not of good and evil. Having heard of good and evil, having seen the sun and moon, those who do not awaken are like vines clinging to a tree: as the tree grows, so do they. When the tree falls, what will the vines cling to?

Today, the assembly of this Daoist sanctuary, as the scriptures warn, trembles in fear and sorrow. Now, with diligence, we bow in repentance, seeking mercy. May we, life after life, never encounter such places. May all beings in hells, hungry ghosts, and animal realms alike attain liberation.

The repentant one, [Name], prostrates for peace and offers this repentance text, throwing himself to the ground with utmost sincerity. With reverence, he bows to the Merciful Honored One and venerates the true and sacred.

With devoted heart, he bows to the Jade Clarity Heavenly Worthy Who Bestows Blessings.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy Who Saves at the Sound of Suffering.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Ascendant Immortals.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Lofty and Unsurpassed Heavenly Worthy.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Compassion and Love.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Constant Mercy.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of No Coming and No Going.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy Who Universally Shelters All.

With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Good Fruits in the Six Paths.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Clarity and Numinous Transformation.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Supreme Clarity and Constant Serenity.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Unity Who Saves from Suffering.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Guards the Realm.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Wishes.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Expanse.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit and Virtue.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Perfected of Orthodox Unity.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Perfected Who Attends the Scriptures.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Saves from Suffering.
With devoted heart, he bows to the Perfected of Great Mercy Who Removes Transgressions.

Today, the patrons of this Daoist ritual and all the assembly reverently pray that the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Northeast, all the Venerables and Sages, all the Great Perfected, all the Great Realized Ones, all the Great Dragon Spirits, all the Great Worthies and Sages, and all the Great Divine Youths—throughout the ten directions and the boundless expanse of the Mysterious Void, all the Perfected and Sages—by the power of great compassion, the power of repentance rites, the power of merit and virtue, and the power of inconceivable efficacy, may grant that the repentance sponsor, so-and-so, their parents of this and past lives, all their relatives by blood and marriage, and their living and deceased kin—those who have passed on, if they suffer in hell for their transgressions—through this act of repentance, be liberated.

We further pray that the Merciful Honored One may manifest the power of goodness to eradicate from the Fengdu Avīci Hell of Uninterrupted Suffering:
the karmic retribution of falling upon knife mountains and sword trees, where limbs and bodies are severed;
the karmic retribution of boiling cauldrons and burning coals, where bodies are scorched and cooked;
the karmic retribution of iron beds and bronze pillars, where bodies are seared and charred;
the karmic retribution of blade wheels and fire chariots, where thunderous bolts strike;
the karmic retribution of having tongues plowed and bodies harrowed, where agony is unbearable;
the karmic retribution of swallowing molten iron pellets and having molten bronze poured into the mouth, where bones and flesh dissolve and rot;
the karmic retribution of being pounded and ground into dust, where bodies are reduced to ashes;
the karmic retribution of having limbs and joints torn apart;
the karmic retribution of wading through filthy ash rivers, where torment and suffocation prevail;
the karmic retribution of enduring saltwater and freezing ice, where skin splits and flesh cracks;
the karmic retribution of being mauled by tigers, wolves, eagles, and hounds, where mutual destruction occurs;
the karmic retribution of being clawed and slashed by blade mountains, where bodies are torn and pierced;
the karmic retribution of being roasted in fire pits, crushed between grinding stones, where bodies are shattered;
the karmic retribution of darkness and confinement, where flesh mountains are carved, bodies are sawed, twisted, and nailed, and limbs are severed;
the karmic retribution of being hung upside down with iron rods, where bodies are butchered and burned, and cries of anguish resound;
the karmic retribution of the great and small Iron Enclosures, the thirty-seven cities, where the three luminaries are unseen, and the sounds *apapa*, *apavava*, *ataṭa*, *ararara* echo—the sufferings of the eight cold and eight hot hells;
the karmic retribution of all the hells, where iron hooks drag bodies, tendons are pulled, intestines are torn, flesh is sliced, and bones are shaved—countless agonies;
may all these karmic retributions be eradicated.

May the kings, their retinues, and all beings receive the moisture of the Dharma and together attain promotion and reward. May all our kin—those not related by blood yet closer than kin—after the breath of life has ceased, whether they have entered these hells or not, by the power of this repentance for karmic transgressions, ascend to the Heavenly Paradise and take refuge in the Great Dao.

One bow.

*Repentance of the Nine Dark Realms, Third Scroll*

Today, all in this Daoist ritual assembly, each with focused mind, reverently face the Merciful Honored One to repent for the sufferings of the Nine Dark Hells in the Nine Dark Realms. The repentance sponsor, so-and-so, gathers their thoughts, kneels in devotion, and listens attentively to the scriptural words.

The Nine Dark Realms lie in the northeast, the land of yin and darkness. Beneath the nine ramparts is the Nine Dark Hell, deep and sunken, where beings are bound and confined.

In the east is the Wind and Thunder Hell, where black winds and thunderous bolts ceaselessly strike, and flying spears and halberds pierce through. The bodies of the condemned are torn apart, and for ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the south is the Fire Obscuration Hell, where the condemned swallow fire and devour coals, scorched by flames. Their heads and faces are charred and rotting, fire mountains rest upon their crowns, and their skin, flesh, and bones blaze in every joint. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the west is the Vajra Hell, where the condemned are beaten with countless iron hammers and rods. Their limbs rot and disintegrate, tendons and bones scatter, iron forks pierce their bellies, and golden hammers lodge in their hearts. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the north is the Dark and Cold Hell, where the condemned sink into freezing pools. Ice spears and frost blades sever their tendons and bones, and the juices of a hundred poisons are poured upon them. Their bodies disintegrate, and their hearts and bellies rupture. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the center is the Universal Torment Hell, where the condemned endure unbearable pain from beatings. Their tendons snap, blood flows, and they collapse in suffocating agony. Then, the hell wardens impale them with iron forks, forcing them to ascend blade mountains and sword trees, where winds from eight directions sway the trees. Their feet tread upon blade mountains, and their bodies are impaled upon sword edges. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the southeast is the Bronze Pillar Hell, where great fires rage with fierce flames. The condemned embrace and climb the pillars, their outer and inner bodies charred and rotting, their backs and bellies oozing pus. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the southwest is the Butchery Hell, where the condemned are hung upside down, their bodies sliced by blades. Their four limbs, tendons, veins, skin, and five viscera are all cut by knives. Blood flows from their bodies, pooling upon the ground, the pain unbearable. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the northwest is the Fire Chariot Hell, where the condemned are torn apart by five chariots, their limbs scattered. Some are placed within the chariots, which drag them east and west. All wheels are edged with blades, and as they turn, they slice the condemned. Fierce fires burn their bodies to cinders. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

In the northeast is the Boiling Cauldron Hell, where the condemned are impaled by iron forks and cast into cauldrons.

Their five bodily parts are boiled and simmered, their four limbs fester and dissolve, pus and blood reek with foulness—unbearable torment. For ten thousand kalpas, they suffer without respite, day and night.

Pǔjì asked, “What grave offenses condemn one to such torment? And who presides over their unceasing interrogation?”

The Compassionate One replied, “Those who commit the three karmic transgressions—slandering the Great Vehicle, disloyalty to the sovereign, maligning monastics, defiling the Dharma-body, destroying sacred images, or embezzling monastic property—fall into the Nine Dark Hells to endure this retribution. There, the Three Officials govern the Nine Bureaus, where clerks and magistrates conduct inquiries, extending even to Fengdu.”

Pǔjì asked, “Is each transgression met with a single punishment, or are a hundred offenses met with a hundred torments?”

The Compassionate One replied, “Iron beds and bronze pillars, agony unbearable—crushed bones and scorched sinews repay the sin of lust. Freezing cold that sears to the bone, forcing them to lie in icy rivers, repays the sin of theft. Molten copper poured into their mouths, tongues torn out and plowed, eyes pecked by vile birds. Sword trees splay their limbs, grinding mills pulverize them like grain—this repays the sin of deceitful glances. Their bodies become hungry ghosts, wandering through cauldrons of boiling liquid, forced to swallow iron pellets when hunger strikes—this repays the sin of breaking precepts. Each interrogation and torment corresponds precisely to their karma, with no discrepancy.

Today, in this ritual space, the penitent, [Name], prostrates in reverence, vowing to dedicate merit with diligence. May the anguish of the Nine Dark Hells be repented, and may all karmic retribution destined for them today be wholly dissolved. The penitent, [Name], bows in devotion, invoking blessings for peace, and recites this repentance text, prostrating with full sincerity, listening with undivided mind.

We bow in reverence to the Compassionate One, honoring the True and Sacred.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Purity who bestows blessings.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who rescues suffering upon hearing cries.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Transcendent Immortals.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of keen wisdom.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of boundless wisdom.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Natural Great Perfection.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of unimpeded divine power.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who parts the darkness with radiant features.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy, the Dharma King of luminous purity.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of compassionate countenance who rescues suffering.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who delivers and transcends life.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who illuminates the Nine Dark Hells.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who delights in practicing the Dao.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who benefits through the Dharma.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ten Thousand Perfected.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of supreme radiance.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Unity who rescues suffering.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who grants longevity and preserves life.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of universal compassion who protects the realm.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of carefree joy.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy who grants rebirth according to vows.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy of boundless expanse.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Heavenly Worthy, Ocean of Merit.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Perfected of the Great Ultimate.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Perfected of Liberation.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Perfected of Great Compassion who rescues suffering.
With devoted hearts, we bow to the Perfected of Great Mercy who absolves transgressions.

Today, the patrons of this ritual space and the great assembly pray to the Heavenly Worthy of the Supreme Numinous Treasure in the northeast, and to all the Venerable Ones, all the Great Perfected, and all the Divine Youths—may they, who pervade the ten directions, the farthest reaches of the cosmos, and all the True and Sacred, radiate their perfect light to illuminate the dark prisons. May destruction be eradicated, and all attain purity. May all suffering souls transcend to the Land of Ultimate Bliss. May blade mountains and sword trees transform into jeweled forests, cauldrons and furnaces into lotus blossoms. May ox-headed jailers become benevolent companions, and all ghosts and spirits abandon malevolent thoughts.

Through this repentance ritual, may all imprisoned in the earth prisons be absolved. May the six paths and four modes of birth awaken to non-action and ascend the true Dao. One bow.

**Chapter Four: Absolving Hell-Prisons, Delivering Hungry Ghosts and Animals**

Today, in this ritual space, each member of the great assembly directs their mind, gazing up to the Compassionate One, arousing compassion and cultivating equanimity. May all officials of the hells be elevated, and may hungry ghosts, animals, and beings in the evil destinies be delivered.

The penitent, [Name], kneels in reverence, concentrating their thoughts, prostrating in repentance. Moreover, the ox-headed jailers, rākṣasas, yakṣas, and countless malevolent ghosts dwelling in hell have yet to transcend the cycle of rebirth. Adrift in the vast sea of suffering, confined in the dark prisons, they have no refuge, forever shrouded in gloom. There are also copper dogs, iron birds, iron horses, iron snakes, iron donkeys, iron oxen, stinking turtles, fierce beasts, venomous insects, and all manner of evil beings—each repaying past misdeeds, bound by karmic retribution.

Today, through this repentance ritual, we vow to universally dedicate our thoughts, relying on the power of goodness, the power of the Dao, and the power of merit. May all officials of the hells attain liberation, escape the realm of suffering, and gradually ascend to the ranks of celestial immortals, reuniting with the supreme Dao. May their karmic fruits transform, and may they be reborn as humans. May all venomous beings self-destruct.

Moreover, those in the realm of hungry ghosts endure eternal hunger and thirst. Though they crave to devour mountains, they never hear the names of broth or water, food or drink, and instead consume pus, blood, and foulness. When their bodies move, their limbs ignite with fire. Their bellies swell like drums, their necks thin as bowstrings.

Today, through this repentance ritual, we vow with boundless thoughts, relying on the power of merit, the inconceivable power, and the power of deliverance. May all hungry ghosts and their kin attain rebirth, receive human form, and enjoy exquisite food and drink that arrive at their wish.

Moreover, those in the animal realm—all species, devoid of knowledge and freedom—endure whipping, torture, slaughter, and butchery. Some have feet, scales, wings, or hooves; some fly, some walk; some have fur, shells, horns, or claws; some are large, some small; some are eaten by humans, others are not. Aquatic creatures, wriggling beings, those born from wombs, eggs, moisture, or transformation—all such kinds.

Through the power of this Daoist ritual arena, the power of repentance rites, and the power of merit, may they attain rebirth in the human realm. The repentant patron [Name] prostrates for peace and offers posthumous deliverance, fearing the karmic causes that may lead to downfall. Relying on this repentance, may all be fully liberated.

The repentant patron [Name] prostrates with five limbs to the ground, wholeheartedly invoking. Bowing in reverence to the Merciful Venerable One, paying homage to the true sages:

With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Clarity who bestows blessings.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Immediate Response who saves from suffering.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Transcendent Immortality.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Ascension through the Nine Grades.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who universally nourishes all beings.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who washes away stagnation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Cyclic Transformation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Radiance.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who verifies fruition.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who delivers from calamity.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Manifest Transformation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Mystic Wisdom.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who propagates the Dao.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Supreme Mystery.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who opens the gate of life.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Manifest Transformation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who apportions rebirth.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Void and Nine Essences.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Unity who saves from suffering.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Longevity and Life Preservation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Bliss.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Rebirth according to Aspiration.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion who protects the realm.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Extent.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy, Ocean of Merit.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Perfected of Universal Salvation.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Perfected of Wondrous Conduct.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Perfected of Great Compassion who saves from suffering.
With devout heart, I pay homage to the Perfected of Great Mercy who absolves transgressions.

Today, the patrons of this ritual arena and the great assembly, looking up in hope, invoke the Supreme Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Northeast, all the venerable ones and sages, all the great immortals of the Five Peaks, the immortals of watery abysses and grottoes, the worthies and sages of altars and earthly domains, all dragon deities and local earth gods throughout the ten directions, to the farthest reaches of the boundless void, all the infinite true sages bearing countless titles.

May all invoke the power of aspiration, the power of vast vows, the power of repentance rites, the power of merit, the boundless and infinite power, so that the repentant patron [Name]’s nine generations of ancestors, three lifetimes of kin, those who have relinquished or received bodies—whether in the hells, the realm of hungry ghosts, or the animal realm, yet to attain liberation—may, through this repentance, achieve transcendence and rebirth, attaining carefree freedom. Through this wondrous power and the power of the Dao, may it extend to all beings, that together they may embrace the mystic wind and ascend the Great Dao.

One bow.

**Section Five: Liberation from Harm Caused by Womb-Birth**

Today, within this sacred precinct, all assembled turn their minds in devotion, prostrating before the Supreme Numinous Treasure’s Compassionate Savior of Suffering in the ten directions, to dissolve and release the calamities of womb-birth and harm inflicted upon others.

The repentant patron [Name], gathering their heart in reverence, kneels and listens attentively, invoking this aspiration:

For the harm of womb-birth is inherited across generations—ancestral customs of worshipping ghosts and spirits, immersion in worldly defilements, and the proliferation of deceit and transgression. Thus, sins accumulate like mountains, summoning severe retribution. In recent years, affairs have been fraught with misfortune, entangled in illness and suffering, with unceasing calamities. Frightening dreams arise in profusion, and strange omens manifest without end. Since ancient times, the afflictions of ancestors have never ceased.

Whether from the three generations of great-grandparents, seven generations of ancestors, nine lineages of kin, or the three lifetimes of parents—both maternal and paternal—if ancestral tombs remain unsettled, they may harbor litigious spirits or malevolent ghosts, their baleful influence unbroken. Or perhaps in burial, construction, relocation, or renovation; in marriage rites or the selection of inauspicious days and hours; in violating taboos; or in excavating pits and trenches, disturbing earth spirits—such acts may subject the living and the dead to torment and punishment, binding their souls in confinement. The misfortunes thus incurred flow onward, extending even to future generations. The transgressions committed are too numerous to recount.

Today, with utmost devotion, we perform this repentance rite, beseeching the Three Saints with sorrowful sincerity, that through this liberation, the repentant patron [Name] may attain deliverance.

Prostrating in reverence for peace and to offer this repentance text, the patron [Name] bows with body and mind, earnestly invoking the Compassionate Savior, paying homage to the True Saints:

With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Jade Clarity Sacred Realm.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Ascended Immortals.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Golden Palace and Jade Treasure.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Three Pristine Forces.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Divine Transformation and Dao’s Workings.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Nine Natural Perfected Ones.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Wondrous Gathering in Golden Clouds.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Radiant Illumination, Dharma Kings.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Golden Form, Serene and Profound.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of a Hundred Billion Manifested Bodies.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Natural Golden Perfected Ones.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Mystic Penetration and Universal Awakening.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Three Origins, Keepers of Records.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Three Caverns, Profound and Still.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Supreme Mystery, Wondrous and Victorious.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Illuminating Response and True Realization.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Liberation from the Four Delusions.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Supreme Unity’s Savior of Suffering.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Longevity and Life Preservation.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Universal Compassion and Nation-Protection.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of Boundless Extent.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Heavenly Worthies of the Ocean of Merit.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Perfected One of Serene Emptiness.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Perfected One of Serene Wisdom.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Great Compassionate Savior of Suffering.
With devoted heart, we bow to the Great Merciful Redeemer of Sins.

Today, the repentant patron and all assembled in this sacred precinct humbly beseech the Supreme Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthies of the northeast, along with all the Venerable Saints, Great Perfected Ones, and Divine Youths—spanning the ten directions, the boundless void, past and future, all hidden and manifest True Saints.

Through the power of the Great Dao-heart, the power of non-action, the power of merit, and the power of supreme goodness, may the three generations of the repentant patron [Name]’s souls—whether lost to famine, banditry, or warfare; to blades, ropes, or unjust imprisonment; to tigers, wolves, or poisonous curses; to bewitchment by trees or stones; to fire, drowning, or self-inflicted wounds; to hanging, epidemics, or the five poisons; to ulcers, leprosy, abscesses, or festering sores; to madness, starvation, or freezing; to sudden malevolent forces or murder by evil spirits; to childbirth complications or miscarriage; to attacks by birds of prey or foxes; or to injuries from livestock—those confined in celestial prisons or earthly hells, bearing sand on their backs or stones upon their shoulders, hauling mountains or filling rivers, enduring ceaseless toil and suffering—be liberated.

Or perhaps their tombs and burial grounds were disturbed, graves opened, coffins desecrated, bones scattered and exposed, skulls and limbs strewn apart, left unburied in the wild, their souls adrift without refuge. Through the power of this virtuous act, may the three generations of souls, long departed, find rest: if their bones lie in water, may they be water-buried; if in fire, fire-buried; if on earth, exposed to the elements; if devoured by beasts, hidden in concealment; if upon wood or stone, entrusted to their care; if slain by blades, transformed by the sword.

May the repentant patron [Name], from this day forward, be freed from misfortune, illness, and suffering; may nightmares cease, and omens vanish. May ancestral souls and tombs forever know peace and prosperity, their households flourishing, sons and daughters thriving, receiving blessings and office, with descendants succeeding in unbroken lineage. May glory and nobility endure across generations, ever upheld by the profound grace of the Dao.

One bow.

The Eighth Scroll of the *Tai Shang’s Compassionate Daoist Ritual for Dispelling Disasters and the Nine Dark Realms* concludes.
The Ninth Scroll of the *Tai Shang’s Compassionate Daoist Ritual for Dispelling Disasters and the Nine Dark Realms* begins.
Compiled by Ge Xuan, the Left Immortal of the Great Ultimate.

**First Chapter: Praying for the State**

Today, the assembly of this Daoist ritual, each with focused mind, gazes reverently toward the Compassionate Honored One. May you expound for all beings, teaching them to pray for the state and their households, seeking grace and blessings.

The repentant patron [Name], kneeling with hands clasped, listens attentively to the scriptural words. If the sovereign faces calamity—celestial bodies losing their course, wars erupting on all sides, winds and rains unbalanced, the hundred grains failing to ripen, the people stricken by plague, the land unsettled, armies mobilized for campaigns, or any manner of disasters and inauspicious omens—all must be reported to me.

Great merits shall be cultivated: transcribing scriptures and commissioning sacred images, establishing temples to deliver beings, and offering from the treasury precious treasures, jewels, gold, silver, pearls, coral, amber, palace gardens, silken banners, fields, gardens, and dwellings. These shall be dedicated as alms, sown into the field of the Three Treasures, to deliver sentient beings, rescue those in peril, release prisoners, establish fasts and precepts, arrange hundreds of high seats, and expound the profound and wondrous teachings of the Great Vehicle. Thus shall the people of the realm be exhorted to listen to the Dharma, practice almsgiving and repentance, and accumulate boundless, inconceivable merits of salvation and protection.

If the sovereign and ministers indulge in wrath, pursue depravity, slaughter without restraint, seek self-indulgence, and oppress all beings, bringing forth calamities upon the people—where sun and moon lose their brightness, baleful stars encroach upon the imperial throne, the land suffers floods and droughts, omens and locusts appear, the people rebel, and usurpers rise—then the sovereign and all under heaven must summon the Three Caverns’ Dharma Bodies and the assembly of the altar, countless in number, to fill sacred altars, temples, mountains, waters, grottoes, and holy sites. There, grand rituals shall be established, banners and canopies hung, flowers scattered, incense burned, lamps lit, the Dao practiced day and night, repentance offered without weariness, and the six periods observed with diligence. Treasures shall be widely dispensed to rescue all beings. Then, by my Dao-power, I shall manifest great divine transformations to assist in dispelling these disasters, causing the afflictions to dissolve at once.

If within the realm the Five Stars lose their proper course, dim luminaries stray, the Twenty-Eight Constellations deviate from their domains, sun and moon suffer eclipses, and yin and yang fall out of harmony, then the Southern Director of Destinies, Lord Han the Venerable, and the Controller of the Eight Directions of the Celestial Sphere, Sima the Longevous, shall regulate the celestial mechanism, restoring them to their rightful positions, and all calamitous omens shall be extinguished.

If great drought leaves the people parched and suffering, then the Dragon Kings shall shake thunder and summon torrential rains to end the drought’s hardship. If heavy rains pour unceasingly, floods surge to the heavens, and the people drown, then the Jade Maiden of the River, the Dark Lord of the Nine Seas, and the Officers of the True Qi shall gather the water-qi, part the clouds, and halt the rain, causing the waters to recede without harm. At this time, all dragon-spirits and ghosts shall likewise turn toward goodness.

If external demons, evil spirits, or malevolent ghosts—*chimei* and *wangliang*—enter the land to spread sickness and suffering, they shall be expelled together, allowed no respite. By the weight of my compassion and virtue, the imperial domain shall be eternally secured, the sovereign’s power ever renewed. The people shall ascend to the court of benevolence and longevity, the state placed within the realm of Huaxu. Yin and yang shall harmonize, sun and moon shine eternally, the seas and lands know peace, ministers and people enjoy well-being, the three frontiers remain tranquil, and the five grains flourish abundantly.

Yet, among the people of the world, though their wealth, status, and conditions differ, even if they cultivate the Dao, they may not discern the proper path. They may perform deeds yet remain beset by calamities, wavering in doubt, unable to attain clarity. They wonder: does the merit of salvation and protection vary in degree?

The Compassionate Honored One replied: Salvation and deliverance from distress depend upon utmost sincerity; the almsgiving of wealth is not measured by quantity. There are five kinds of merit:

First, the creation of my sacred images—true, responsive, and transformative manifestations. Blessings shall flow across kalpas, and retribution shall be boundless. Why? Because sentient beings, lost in delusion, cannot fix their minds. Beholding my true form, they generate devotion. With devotion arisen, true numen descends to meet them. Focused and unwavering, they attain the fruit of non-action.

Second, the transcription of scriptural teachings—the Great Vehicle of the Three Caverns. Blessings shall flow eternally, and merits shall be immeasurable. For scriptures guide the deluded, awakening boundless Dao-mind in beings, leading them from confusion to enlightenment, from enlightenment to truth. All sages who cultivate the Dao ascend to its fruition.

Third, the establishment of temples to deliver beings, the construction of halls and sanctuaries. The merit is boundless, inconceivable. Why?

Third, the deliverance of beings through monastic ordination and temple stewardship, the propagation of scriptures and icons to teach and transform sentient beings, inspiring them to awaken the Dao-mind—one realization opening myriad gates. Through the turning of karmic conditions, they aid the nation and transform the people, spreading the Dao and illuminating the Dharma, yielding the greatest benefit.

Fourth, the observance of purification rites and the practice of the Dao, the performance of repentance and the recitation of scriptures, the offering of praise and the burning of incense. The field of merit is boundless. Thus, purification rites cleanse the heart, the Dao enables penetrating insight, the practice of the Dao atones for transgressions, repentance invokes blessings, and the resonance of merit moves the heavens, dispelling calamities and bestowing fortune, upon which both life and death depend.

Fifth, the bestowal of all things in boundless fields of merit. The karmic retribution is towering, its merit profound and deep. Wealth and possessions are the lifeblood of sentient beings, clung to as if one’s own life, yet to relinquish them without hesitation, to give without stinginess, is to broadly establish merit, universally succoring sentient beings, inwardly stilling greed and avarice, outwardly eliminating plunder and theft. In life and death, they receive grace, and both humans and heavens reap the benefit.

These five Dharma-gates of merit-making are to be cultivated gradually according to one’s capacity, safeguarding the nation and securing the household, transcending rebirth and delivering from suffering. As the scriptures say, it is like a single sweet rain—all who receive it are nourished. According to their innate faculties, each attains flourishing growth. So too is the performance of repentance and the seeking of forgiveness.

Today, the assembly of this Dao-field, having heard the scriptural teachings, exhorts sentient beings to establish these inconceivable merits. The repentant one, so-and-so, from kalpas without beginning until this very kalpa and this present life, has never before encountered such merit or the analogies of these Dharma-gates. Today, prostrating for peace and offering this repentance text in ancestral veneration, they attain great awakening and understanding, bowing with utmost reverence, listening with single-minded devotion.

With bowed heads, they pay homage to the Merciful Venerable One, reverently saluting the true sages:
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Jade Purity Heavenly Worthy, Bestower of Fortune.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Rescues from Suffering at the Sound of Cries.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Jade Void Radiant August Heavenly Worthy.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Supreme Ultimate’s True Form.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of True Unity and Spontaneity.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Records All.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Transformative Qi.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Dragon Virtue.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Victorious Countenance.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Lofty Virtue.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Mystery.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Joyful Wandering.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Eight Poles.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Knows the True.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Five Qi.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Void.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Pure Emptiness.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Golden Countenance.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Responds to Devotion.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Jade Capital.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Protects and Responds.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Great One Who Rescues from Suffering.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Guards the Nation.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Wishes.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Boundless Heavenly Worthy.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Perfected One of Precious Countenance.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Perfected One of Perfect Quiescence.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Perfected One of Great Compassion Who Rescues from Suffering.
With devoted heart, they reverently salute the Perfected One of Great Compassion Who Eradicates Transgressions.

Today, the repentant one of this Dao-field, together with the great assembly, surrenders and takes refuge, reverently beseeching the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Upper Realm, all the Venerables and Sages, all the Great Heavenly Immortals, all the Immortals of the Great Grotto-Heavens, Earth Immortals, Water Immortals, Flying Immortals, Perfected Ones of Universal Salvation, Perfected Ones Who Rescue from Suffering, Youths Who Rescue from Suffering, and all true sages throughout the ten directions, the farthest reaches of the mysterious void, and all realms manifest and hidden.

May their vast and mysterious grace universally flow through the land. May the emperor’s reign be eternally prolonged, the beacon fires of war unlit, weapons stilled and sheathed, borders secured and frontiers guarded. May the imperial princes and heirs together strengthen the imperial enterprise, ministers and officials loyal and upright, assisting counselors and chancellors sharing the nation’s prosperity, jointly upholding the cosmos.

May heaven and earth be bright and pure, the celestial signs clear and mysterious, floods and droughts forever dispelled, locusts and pests never arise. May the three frontiers know perpetual peace, disasters and epidemics sink into obscurity, wind and rain arrive in season, harvests be abundant in years of plenty. May heaven bestow sweet dew, earth bring forth auspicious clouds, the nation prosper with worthy ministers, households abound with filial piety and fraternal duty.

Next, may the prisons of Mount Luofeng, the eight difficulties and nine dark realms, cease their torments, and the suffering souls forever escape the three evil destinies.

The repentant one, so-and-so, from kalpas without beginning until this present kalpa and life, together with nine generations of ancestors, parents, and all kin, by the power of this repentance and merit, may all attain liberation and return to the true Dao.

One bow.

**Second Scroll: The Salvation of the People**

Today, in this grand Daoist sanctuary, all present turn their minds upward, gazing toward the Merciful Honored One, to broadly save the people and expound all virtuous benefits.

The repentant one, so-and-so, gathers their thoughts, joins their hands, and listens attentively to the scriptural words, ever mindful of sentient beings dwelling in an age of the three poisons and ten evils, beset by specters and malevolent spirits, wicked ghosts and wayward deities, venomous creatures and fierce beasts, blades and warfare, flood and fire, fetters and prisons, sickness and suffering—each affliction clinging fast, leaving none at peace.

Thus are the Three Caverns’ scriptures and precepts expounded, the rites of deliverance and purification performed, to universally ferry all beings across. Talismans, sacred diagrams, and divine incantations are entrusted to those who study the Dao, along with the Heavenly Emperors, the Saviors of Suffering Perfected Ones, the Three Great Demon Kings of Heaven, and the Five Demon Kings of Heaven, who spread throughout the world to rescue and protect all, granting them freedom.

Yet sentient beings, deluded and ignorant, fail to recognize sin and blessing. They indulge the six senses, killing and stealing, engaging in debauchery and dissipation, stinginess and wrath, their natures inverted. They speak deceitfully, utter falsehoods, slander with harsh words and divisive tongues, devour living beings, break fasts and violate precepts, defy heaven and betray earth, turn from the true and embrace the perverse, curse gods and spirits—sins rampant, with not a shred of goodness.

Thus do poisonous winds and malignant qi, the demonic hordes of the Six Heavens, fill the world, spreading slaughter and strife. Those struck down and wounded number in the tens of thousands each day, beyond all reckoning.

The Merciful Honored One dispatches the Heavenly Emperors, the Ten Ultimate Divine Kings, and the Four Administrators of the Three Realms to descend into the human realm, traversing and rescuing, delivering sentient beings, filling heaven and earth—yet who among them knows this?

Now I solemnly declare to you: the methods of salvation are inconceivable, their spiritual responses swift. In universal deliverance, I proclaim with great compassion and mercy, entreating the Honored One to bestow these teachings.

The Merciful Honored One says: On the first day of the year, the eight solar terms, the Three Primes, the dark and full moons, the Five La Days, and the Ten Straight Days—on all such occasions, good men and faithful women who observe these days must abstain from meat and impurity, restrain the six senses, and banish all wayward thoughts. Thus purified, they burn incense, maintain the fast, recite the Dao, and pay homage to my transformed names.

First, they repent for their own transgressions, openly confessing their faults, thereby transferring merit to amend their errors and escape suffering and calamity. If one cannot focus alone, they may invoke the Dharma-bodies of male or female officiants, praying earnestly with devotion, making offerings and prostrations.

Whether at home or in sacred temples, with flowers, fruits, vegetarian meals, banners, blossoms, incense, lamps, and offerings of clothing, bedding, curtains, embroidered mats, fragrant oils, rice, and flour—whatever they possess—then the benevolent spirits will descend at once, delivering them from misfortune.

If one suffers from grave illness, chronic ailments, or the malevolent influence of the Ox Mansion, lingering for years without relief, their vitality drained, their wealth dissipated; if childbirth brings misfortune, or infants perish in their arms; if one leaves the household to become a monastic, only to later regret it; if nightmares and strange visions disturb the mind, or fires and alarms cause terror; if legal troubles arise unjustly, or one violates sacred prohibitions, defies divine retribution, disturbs graves, or is struck by flood, fire, entangling trees, or crushing stones—all manner of calamities, omens, and afflictions—then within the home, perform extensive rites of repentance and supplication. According to one’s means, pay homage to my transformed names, kindle lamps and burn incense day and night without cease. The Four Heavenly Emperor-Kings will descend to protect my transformed names.

The exorcised will be subdued, the sought will be granted, the presented will be conveyed, the entreated will be heeded. Transgressions will be redeemed, the living and the dead will be saved. This form of prayer and exorcism is foremost.

If emperors, kings, great ministers, and royal advisors, along with princes, consorts, imperial children, and celestial descendants, act on behalf of their parents, themselves, their kin, court relatives, and imperial kin, summoning the Dharma-bodies of male and female officiants—regardless of number—to their palaces, where they maintain the fast, practice the Dao, and perform repentance day and night without pause, their devotion unwavering, then the Ten Perfected Ones of Heaven and the Four Administrators and Five Emperors will descend to assess their merits and faults. The sick will recover, the dead will revive, the imperiled will be delivered, the imprisoned will be freed, travelers will return, and officials will be promoted. Water, fire, blades, warfare, tigers, wolves, venomous beasts, malevolent spirits, and spectral entities will never assail them, nor will they suffer harm or offense.

If common folk act on behalf of emperors, kings, the people, the land, and all sentient beings, paying homage to my transformed names and true images, delivering all beings, each will attain peace and bliss—this is most inconceivable.

If warfare erupts on all four fronts, encroaching upon borders, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and the weapons of war will retreat, leaving no harm or damage.

If plague and pestilence strike the people, and exorcisms bring no relief, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and the afflicted will recover, free from lingering illness.

If floods and droughts disrupt the seasons, and the five grains fail to ripen, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and the elements will harmonize, all things flourishing.

If poisonous winds and malignant qi scorch the people, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and the afflictions will vanish at once, the body and qi restored to tranquility.

If venomous creatures and fierce beasts ravage the people and all living beings, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and the insects and tigers will flee, the mountain spirits concealing them.

If a woman is pregnant and childbirth brings peril, pay homage to my transformed names and true images, and mother and child will be reunited, free from danger.

Ten thousand disasters will vanish, a thousand transformations and myriad changes will cease. Turn to me, to my transformed names, who broadly protect all sentient beings—no wish will go unfulfilled. With sincere devotion, no peril will remain unaverted.

Today, in this grand Daoist sanctuary, all present must turn their minds as the scriptures instruct, with utmost devotion, paying homage to all transformed names and manifestations.

May these merits and virtues broadly deliver all sentient beings, universally ferry them across to liberation. The repentant sponsor, so-and-so, has dwelt in the world since time immemorial, sunk in the depths of sin and suffering, yet to attain liberation. Today, prostrating for peace and offering this repentance text, they cast themselves to the ground with utmost reverence, wholeheartedly invoking the names. Bowing their head to the Merciful Venerable One, they pay homage to the true sages:

With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Clarity who bestows blessings.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who rescues from suffering at the sound of distress.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Void and Luminous Sovereignty.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who venerates immortals and protects life.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Might and Virtue.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Mystic Quiescence.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Bodily Liberation.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who propagates the Teaching.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who pacifies dragons.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Central Dharma.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Constant Serenity.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who flourishes the Dao.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Myriad Wonders.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Tenuity.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of True Appearance.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Dharma.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Immeasurable Life.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who upholds the Dao and its virtue.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Purple Clarity who descends with blessings.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Mystic Virtue who rescues and delivers.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Perfect and Complete Right Wisdom.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who responds to conditions in all directions.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Unity who rescues from suffering.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Longevity who preserves life.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion who protects the realm.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Reach.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who is the Ocean of Merit and Virtue.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who grants rebirth according to one’s wishes.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Perfected One of Equal Illumination.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Perfected One of Jade Radiance.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Perfected One of Great Compassion who rescues from suffering.
With devoted heart, they pay homage to the Perfected One of Great Mercy who absolves sins.

Today, the patrons of this Daoist sanctuary, together with the great assembly, bow their heads in reverence and take refuge, gazing upward in hope that the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy, all the venerable ones and sages, all the great flying immortals, celestial immortals, terrestrial immortals, aquatic immortals, all the great perfected ones, all the great youths, and all the transformed true images and sacred manifestations throughout the ten directions and the boundless reaches of the Mystic Void, will together extend their vast grace, propagate the Mystic Wind, pervade the world, universally succor the multitudes, dispel disasters, and bestow blessings.

May the repentant sponsor, so-and-so, by the power of this Dao, see exorcised what is to be exorcised, preserved what is to be preserved, healed what is ailing, turned auspicious what is dire, liberated the recently deceased, reborn in heaven the long departed, and all sunken and lingering souls ascend through the wheel of karma. May all sentient beings be delivered and saved, depart from the source of suffering, and together ascend the shore of the Dao.

One bow.

**Chapter Three: Unbinding the Knots of Sentient Beings**

Today, within this sacred precinct, all assembled turn their minds in reverence toward the Merciful Honored One, the Boundless Dao, and all true sages, that for the sake of sentient beings, they may untie all knots and fetters.

The repentant sponsor, so-and-so, with purified body and mind, bows in profound devotion. As the scriptures declare: In the beginning, the Primordial One transformed the Three Realms with a single qi. Heaven and earth move, and the myriad things take form; humanity dwells within, receiving its nature and nurturing its form, all born of this transformation. Externally, it draws upon refined qi; internally and externally, the five virtues intermingle to take shape. Sentient beings, enveloped within, emerge from the womb after ten months, encircled by the ten qi. As qi circulates and gives life, the hundred joints unfold. Within each joint, qi forms ten knots, and within each knot resides a spirit. Habitual patterns intertwine, and transgressions coil into bonds.

To untie these knots and harmonize the hundred spirits, the ten directions are established, each bearing countless names. Each invoked name has the power to unbind the knots of sentient beings. If the knots of sentient beings are dissolved, they deeply awaken to the source of the Dao—much like in the worldly realm, where capturing a thief requires summoning a thousand soldiers, yet once the thief is seized, not a single soldier is needed.

Moreover, the body of sentient beings is a temporary convergence of earth, water, fire, and wind, of yin and yang, manifest and hidden, all arising from the mutual contamination of the five viscera and six senses. The mind-king and the will-steed sow and cultivate: knots of doubt and delusion, knots of entanglement and obstruction, knots of injury and harm, knots of illness and affliction, knots of slander and strife, knots of enmity and grievance, knots of chronic ailment, knots of muteness and silence, knots of frivolity and play, knots of trade and exchange, knots of wine and gluttony, knots of killing and harm, knots of scalding and fire, knots of jealousy and envy, knots of false speech, knots of frivolity and disdain, knots of greed and desire, knots of reckless bravery, knots of breaking fasts, knots of violating precepts, knots of idle amusement, knots of mental exhaustion, knots of accumulated resentment, knots of shamelessness, knots of lust and desire, knots of deafness, knots of blindness, knots of mental confusion, knots of anger and rage, knots of heavenly nets, knots of earthly snares, knots of water and fire, knots of the bridal chamber, knots of mutual conflict, knots of mutual hindrance.

All such sentient beings, dwelling within heaven and earth, experience the flourishing and withering of form. The burning house seethes unceasingly; floating life is ever restless. With all these vexing knots obstructing and tormenting the fleshly body, knot upon knot intertwines without end.

Pǔjì inquired: What is meant by the mind-king and the will-steed?

The Merciful Honored One replied: The mind is like a sovereign king; the will is like a monkey or a horse—difficult to tame, difficult to subdue, ever-shifting and unceasing. Even if the monkey and horse are stilled, the mind-king does not rest. If one skillfully subdues the sovereign king, the will-steed cannot shift and turn. Once shifting and turning cease, karmic knots no longer arise.

Pǔjì inquired: By what virtuous power may sentient beings be taught to awaken and dissolve these knots?

The Merciful Honored One replied: If sentient beings seek awakening and dissolution, let them, in a place of purity, adorn and purify their homes. According to their means, whether abundant or modest, let them light incense and lamps before my image, venerate the transformed names, repent of grievances and knots, listen attentively, contemplate deeply, and advance with courage and diligence. Thus may they awaken and dissolve all knots, avoiding the depths of suffering.

By the power of this repentance, let there descend the hundredfold-refined vajra, the thousandfold-blended jade elixir, the flowing light of Venus, the dispersed radiance of primal yellow. Let these wash away lewdness and perversity, dissolve grievances and knots, dispel vexation and torment, pacify body and mind. Let goodness and evil naturally align, and malevolence be ground away. May the Four Brahma Perfected Ones and the transformative lords of the ten directions enable all sentient beings to awaken. Let evil karma not arise, and let goodness deepen, that they may attain rebirth—how could they not be delivered?

Furthermore, if sentient beings skillfully dissolve even a single knot, a hundred knots will loosen. They will ascend in pure qi and descend with heavenly talismans. The fierce generals Axiū, Iron-Forehead, and Copper-Headed Dharma-Protecting Divine Kings, with jade hooks and golden locks, will instantly still the thousand knots and myriad resentments, quieting the mind-monkey. Like an orange or a pearl, the will’s knots will forever cease. The mind will be without mind, and knots without knots. Enmity and hatred will be resolved, nets and snares dissolved.

May all sentient beings forever awaken to the true Dao and attain liberation.

Today, within this sacred precinct, all assembled turn their minds to listen attentively, as the scriptures declare: Sentient beings in the world are forever bound by the cage of affliction, with no means of escape—where can they flee? By venerating this repentance ritual, they may suddenly awaken from their entanglements. Now, let them contemplate deeply and advance in reverent devotion.

May the power of virtue extend to all sentient beings, that all the knots they bear may, by the power of repentance, awaken to non-action and ascend to the true Dao.

The repentant sponsor, so-and-so, further reflects: Dwelling in the floating world, one daily accumulates evil qi. The body bears the three karmic actions; the mouth commits the four transgressions. Karmic roots intertwine, and knots gather, difficult to cast off. Today, let the body be refined and purified, the dust of defilement washed away.

Today, prostrating for peace and offering prayers through this repentance text, with the five limbs touching the earth and the mind single-mindedly devoted, the repentant sponsor bows to the Merciful Honored One and reverently venerates the true sages.

With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Jade Purity Heavenly Worthy who bestows blessings.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who rescues from suffering upon hearing the cry.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Clarity and Luminous Sovereignty.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who establishes merit universally.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who widely propagates the Dao’s allure.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy adorned with meritorious virtue.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who compassionately expounds the Dharma.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Most High’s teachings.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of unfathomable sagely virtue.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy with wondrous golden countenance.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who engenders the four qi.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who verifies fruition and fulfills vows.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy who opens the Dao to rebirth.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Hall of Ten Thousand Blessings.

With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Lofty and Wondrous Dao.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Wise and Virtuous Conduct.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Responsive Manifestation.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Supreme Numinosity.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Dharma Ocean.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Myriad Wonders.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Meritorious Virtue and Luminous Wisdom.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Great One Who Delivers from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Guards the Realm.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Vows.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Extent.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Meritorious Virtue.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Perfected of the Golden Wheel.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Perfected Who Subdues Demons.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Delivers from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, reverently venerate the Perfected of Great Mercy Who Eradicates Transgressions.

Today, the master of repentance in this Daoist ritual, together with the great assembly, prostrate in utmost sincerity, gazing upward in hope that the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Upper Realm, all the Venerables and Sages, all the Great Transformative Titles, all the Great Manifestations, all the Great Divine Immortals, all the Great Assemblies of Sages, all the Great Divine Youths, and all the Worthies and Sages throughout the ten directions and the boundless reaches of the Mysterious Void—all the Perfected and Sages—may, through the might of the Vajra Guardians and the waters of Supreme Harmony, cleanse the accumulated defilements within the body of the repentance master, named so-and-so, purifying the field of the heart-mind. May obstructions dissolve, the flow of nourishing and protective qi circulate, and all share a purified heart-mind, continuously cultivating goodness without generating defiled thoughts or stirring afflictive toil.

Today, this Daoist ritual is conducted with purity as its purpose. May the ancestral spirits, the consciousness of departed kin, parents, and family members swiftly escape karmic entanglements, never to sink into suffering. May the living and the deceased of two generations together ascend to the fruition of the Dao.

One bow.

**Chapter Four: Arousing the Heart of Praise**

Today, in this Daoist ritual, each member of the great assembly directs their heart-mind upward, gazing toward the Compassionate Venerable One, exhorting all beings to arise in praise.

The repentance master, named so-and-so, gathers their heart-mind, kneels in reverence, and listens attentively to the scriptural words: No one receives birth without arising from past karma. Thus, each is endowed with a divine and outstanding nature, each with its own karmic conditions. Transgressions and blessings, fortune and misfortune—all proceed from karma. Therefore, short or long lifespans, nobility or lowliness, wealth or poverty, beauty or ugliness, foolishness or wisdom—each differs according to prior determination. If one knows they have committed the three karmic actions or the ten evils, their transgressions are grave and weighty. They should awaken to remorse, seek repentance, and perform rites of contrition. Let boundless thoughts arise from an immeasurable heart-mind. Whenever encountering good conditions, one must offer praise. The merit of praise is inconceivable.

If one sees the emperor, sovereign, empress, imperial consorts, princes, princesses, ministers, and high officials arouse a heart of great goodness, one must offer praise, wishing that blessings protect the realm and the imperial enterprise endure forever.

If one sees the construction of palaces or the establishment of vast Daoist altars, one must offer praise, wishing for swift completion and the attainment of refuge.
