If one sees the imperial grace bestowing ordination upon male and female officials and Daoists, one must offer praise, wishing for liberation from suffering and purity across three lifetimes.

If one sees the adornment and casting of sacred images, the true responsive and transformative bodies, one must offer praise, arousing a heart of reverence and making offerings without cease.

If one sees the transcription of the Three Caverns’ Great Canon of sacred scriptures, one must offer praise, wishing for eternal circulation and the transformation and deliverance of all.

If one sees halls, pavilions, towers, and terraces adorned with splendor and elegance, one must offer praise, wishing that all may attain refuge and constantly behold and revere them.

If one sees bells, chimes, and Daoist implements of bronze and iron, one must offer praise, wishing to awaken the deluded masses and make their voices heard in the darkest nights.

If one sees the expounding of various scriptures and the elucidation of wondrous meanings, one must offer praise, wishing to ride the merit to liberate those imprisoned in suffering.

If one sees the recitation of scriptures and repentance texts, their upholding, and the making of offerings, one must offer praise, wishing to attain the conditions for the Dao and remain steadfast without retreat.

If one sees the performance of ritual circumambulation, hymns of praise, prayers for blessings, and petitions for fortune, one must offer praise, wishing that the power of blessings universally pervade worlds as numerous as motes of dust.

If one sees men and women burning incense, lighting lamps, and diligently prostrating in reverence, one must offer praise, wishing their prayers be fulfilled.

If one sees the burning of incense, one must offer praise, universally wishing that the fragrant smoke be offered to all Perfected and Sages.

If one sees the illumination of lamps dispelling darkness, one must offer praise, wishing that karmic debts be forever dissolved and all attain equality with the sun and moon.

If one sees the observance of fasts, the upholding of precepts, and the making of offerings to the Perfected and Sages, one must offer praise, wishing that all sentient beings in the world, all creatures with consciousness, forever enter the Dharma gate and never sink into the realms of suffering.

If one sees the making of offerings to humans and gods, one must offer praise, wishing for towering blessings and longevity, and inexhaustible wealth and fortune.

If one sees diligent devotion, thought after thought of utmost sincerity, one must offer praise, wishing for no retreat and constant joy.

If one sees courageous reverence and the arousal of a heart of great goodness, one must offer praise, wishing to avoid encountering demonic obstacles and swiftly attain the true Dao.

If one sees those who dwell at home constantly reciting scriptures and repentance texts, one must offer praise, wishing that all heavenly Perfected may hear and behold them.

If one sees those who dwell in mountains to cultivate the Dao, residing in hermitages and cliffs, guarding their resolve in tranquility, seeking neither fame nor profit, one must offer praise, wishing that those who first attain the Dao may sequentially open the path to deliverance for others.

If one sees men and women of upright bearing, one must offer praise, universally wishing that they leave the household life and perpetuate the true teaching.

If one sees all good conditions in the world, one must offer praise, wishing that humans and gods attain fruition and all receive benefit.

Through such manifold praises of good deeds, exhort and inspire all beings to accomplish the heart-mind of the Dao and enter diligent practice. Thus may the nine generations of ancestors, the seven generations of forebears, one’s own parents, uncles, brothers, oneself, one’s descendants, and all family members—from beginningless kalpas to the present kalpa, in this life and this birth, through the accumulated actions of today—all the heavy transgressions of the three karmic actions, the six sense faculties, the five rebellious acts, and the ten evils be completely dissolved.

Today, the great assembly of this Dao ritual, as proclaimed in the scriptures, must recognize that the power of praising goodness is inconceivable. We must diligently advance, widely offering praise, wishing that this merit universally extend to all sentient beings. The repentance master, so-and-so, prostrates for peace and offers this repentance text in memorial rites, bowing with five limbs to the ground, single-mindedly invoking and reverently saluting the Merciful Honored One and the true sages.

With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Jade Purity Heavenly Worthy Who Bestows Blessings.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy Who Responds to Cries and Relieves Suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Jade Void Radiant August Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Mystery Capital.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Immeasurable Life.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Eternal Stillness and Silence.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Unobstructed Eloquence.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Inconceivable.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Vast Transformation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of True Wisdom.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy Who Initiates Salvation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Appearances.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy Who Expounds True Emptiness.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Wondrous Dharma and Sacred Wisdom.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Mysterious Concealment and Non-Action.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Unfathomable Dark Source.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Wondrous Joy and Universal Salvation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Transformation and Mysterious Radiance.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Illumination and Non-Action.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Mysterious Penetration and Myriad Changes.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy Who Saves According to Merit.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Eight Trigrams Who Protects the Body.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great One Who Relieves Suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Longevity and Life Preservation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Protects the Nation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Joyous Transcendence.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Wishes.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Extent.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Perfected of Equal Radiance.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Perfected of Cyclic Transformation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Relieves Suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Eradicates Transgressions.

Today, the repentance master of this Dao ritual and the great assembly take refuge and aspire toward the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Upper Realm, all the venerable ones and sages, all the gods and immortals of the heavens, all the great dragon spirits and local earth deities, all the great perfected ones, all the great true adepts, and all the divine youths—those who pervade the ten directions, fill the boundless void, and manifest as all true sages. May they, by the power of the great Dao, the power of non-action, the power of merit, and the power of the inconceivable, enable the repentance master, so-and-so, from beginningless kalpas to the present kalpa, in this life and this day, along with the nine generations of ancestors, the seven generations of forebears, teachers, parents, uncles, brothers, oneself, and all family members—both the living and the deceased—who may have encountered various good conditions but failed to offer praise, to have all their transgressions dissolved through this act of repentance.

From this day forward, may we ourselves, upon hearing or seeing any good conditions, rejoice and leap with joy, redoubling our praise, encouraging diligent cultivation, and aspiring to accomplish the universal salvation of all beings. May our nine generations of ancestral spirits, our parents of this life, our teachers and Dharma companions, our fellow practitioners and kin, our uncles, brothers, and all family members—those who have passed away—be freed from karmic obstructions and forever severed from afflictions. May the power of this repentance extend universally, adorning and pacifying the realm, bringing peace to the borders, and even enabling those in hells, hungry ghost realms, and animal existences to equally rely on this profound grace and attain the shore of the Dao.

One bow.

The Ninth Scroll of the *Tai Shang Merciful Dao Ritual for Eliminating Disasters and the Nine Dark Realms* concludes.

The Tenth Scroll of the *Tai Shang Merciful Dao Ritual for Eliminating Disasters and the Nine Dark Realms*

Compiled by Ge Xuan, the Left Immortal Duke of the Great Ultimate

**Chapter One: Manifesting Merit and Receiving Blessings**

Today, the great assembly of this Dao ritual, each directing their mind, respectfully addresses the Merciful Honored One, declaring their merits to receive blessings. The repentance master, so-and-so, joins palms, kneels, and listens attentively to the scriptural teachings.

The Universal Salvation inquires: The various Dharma gates of merit manifested by the Merciful Honored One exhort and instruct sentient beings to cultivate practice. Yet beings are weak and feeble, unable to fully accomplish these; we wonder what levels of merit may be attained through cultivation.

The Merciful Honored One says: Merit is boundless, but broadly speaking, there are nine types, each yielding blessings according to one’s capacity. All beings should listen carefully:

1. Creating images
2. Copying scriptures
3. Establishing temples
4. Liberating beings
5. Conducting Dao rituals
6. Reciting scriptures and performing repentance rites
7. Upholding precepts
8. Universally offering vegetarian feasts and provisions
9. Practicing generosity

Whether constructing halls, pavilions, towers, galleries, permanent estates, banners, flowers, lamps, candles, bells, chimes, cymbals, or other ritual implements—all such endeavors accumulate boundless merit, bringing immeasurable blessings in the past, present, and future, beyond conception.

Those who create images or copy scriptures will, in this life, attain noble status and, in past lives, be reborn in the families of heavenly kings. Those who establish temples and liberate beings will, in this life, attain great wealth and, in past lives, be reborn in the families of kings. Those who perform rituals and recite invocations will, in this life, be protected by benevolent spirits and, in past lives, be reborn with keen intelligence. Those who uphold vegetarian precepts, revere the teachings, and burn incense will, in this life, enjoy enduring peace and, in past lives, be reborn in wealthy and noble families. Those who observe precepts and repent will, in this life, be revered and protected by the gods and, in past lives, be reborn among humans with perfect form and appearance. Those who offer scriptures and images will, in this life, receive good karmic retribution and, in past lives, be reborn with handsome features. Those who offer vegetarian feasts and provisions will, in this life, have abundant clothing and food and, in past lives, be reborn with dignified bearing. Those who give alms to the poor will, in this life, attain radiant perfection and, in past lives, be reborn with auspicious marks.

Those who refrain from consuming living beings will, in this life, enjoy freedom from illness and suffering and, in past lives, attain a long-lived body. Those who abstain from wine and meat will, in this life, have spirits that abide in their bodies and, in past lives, be reborn with the bodies of sages and worthies. Those who are free from craving and content with little will, in this life, have bodies free from foul odors and, in past lives, be reborn with pure bodies. Those who release life and ransom creatures will, in this life, be spared from premature death and, in past lives, be reborn with reverent bodies. Those who expound the teachings and transform others will, in this life, attain the dual cultivation of blessings and wisdom and, in past lives, be reborn with the bodies of renunciates.

Moreover, the retribution of meritorious deeds is like an echo responding to sound, like a shadow following form—no difference in magnitude, purity and turbidity naturally distinct. Yet you, in your ignorance and delusion, fail to recognize causes and conditions, disbelieve in the consequences of sin and merit, and do not understand that this body arises from the seeds of past blessings. You do not know that this body is but a fleeting apparition, that it is utterly illusory, that it is momentary and impermanent. Instead, you indulge in stinginess and greed, killing living beings, stealing, engaging in illicit sex and dissipation, consuming living creatures, uttering deceitful and frivolous speech, slandering the scriptures and teachings, amassing wealth—all the while believing this life has no limit.

Consider all beings: with eyes open, they commit countless sins; with eyes closed, they enter the prison of suffering. A lifetime of transgressions—when have they ever awakened? They cannot arouse a single thought of goodness to disperse the karmic deeds that bind them to past and future rebirths. Though they seek to liberate themselves, they plant the seeds of affliction, yet fret over their descendants, lamenting their lack of sustenance. I grieve for worldly people, who weep at the moment of death, yet from youth are consumed by worry for their sons and daughters, never recalling the kindness of their parents’ nurture. From time without beginning, they have imitated one another, never awakening, ever sinking deeper into ignorance.

I reflect further on all of you, who follow one another in folly, never self-aware. Thus I reveal the karmic causes and conditions of past lives, that you may emerge from the river of suffering and desire. I also lament that sentient beings drift and drown, never escaping the sea of suffering. This world is called the "Realm of Abandoned Worthies and Profit-Seeking," also known as the "Realm of Mixed Retribution." The heavens of desire and attachment arise within it, fleeting as lightning—appearing for a moment, then vanishing; briefly gathering, then scattering. Birth, aging, sickness, death; pain, itching, soreness, aching; hunger, cold, dryness, dampness; water, fire, blades, weapons; demonic spirits, thieves, poisonous winds, malignant diseases—all these afflictions intertwine, moment by moment impermanent, never abiding for even an instant. How much suffering! Yet even as these torments bind you in the present, you remain unaware—how then could you believe in the celestial realms, the blessed lands of immortals, the Dao of eternal life, and the freedom of non-action?

I observe that the lives of worldly beings are shorter than those of mayflies; their dwellings more cramped than a hair’s tip; their foulness more vile than excrement; their pleasures no different from those of dung-beetles. Yet they remain oblivious, mistaking this for happiness—is this not suffering? I further reflect that no one is born without prior karma. Thus, when examining the essence of spirit and form, each has its causes and conditions. Sin and merit, fortune and misfortune—all arise from karma. Therefore, longevity or premature death, nobility or lowliness, wealth or poverty, beauty or ugliness, foolishness or wisdom—each differs according to its kind, even among birds, beasts, insects, fish, chickens, dogs, grasses, and trees. How much more so for human birth, which is so rarely encountered! Once this body decays, when will it be regained after ten thousand kalpas?

Thus I earnestly admonish and exhort you: diligently cultivate precepts, fast, practice the Dao, recite scriptures, prostrate in worship, burn incense, light lamps, give alms, and repent. Vow to deliver the living and liberate the dead; create images and copy scriptures; establish temples and build bridges; dig wells by the roadside to aid travelers and relieve the thirsty. Through countless expedient means, pave the path for all beings in the future. What do I seek in this? All sentient beings should reflect deeply.

Today, in this grand assembly, as the scriptures teach and the Dharma reveals—whether in full or in part, beyond comprehension—we earnestly establish the foundation of blessings for ourselves and others, creating the path for the future. Now, as I bow in reverence and recite, let each of you be diligent. May these merits benefit all without limit, and may every sentient being receive their nourishment.

The repentance master [Name], prostrating for peace and offering this repentance text, prays that these merits respond to the heart’s aspirations. With five limbs touching the earth and a single mind, I vow:

With utmost reverence, I bow to the Compassionate Venerable One.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Jade Clarity Bestower of Blessings, Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Rescues from Suffering at the Sound of Cries.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the True August and Mysterious Spirit.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Everlasting Radiance.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Perfect Dharma-Body.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Purple Cloud Canopy.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Mysterious Wisdom and Distant Illumination.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Profound Stillness and Mysterious Essence.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Disperses Majestic Form.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Responds to Needs.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Transcends Birth and Death.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Radiant Light.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Dao and Qi.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Origin.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Luminous Form.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Realizes the Dao.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Blessings and Longevity.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Manifest Response.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Northern Culmen.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Supreme Heavenly Worthy.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of True Inner Names.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Joyous Primordial Affinity.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Great Unity Who Rescues from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Guards the Nation.

With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Wishes.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Expanse.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit and Virtue.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Universal Salvation.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Universal Compassion.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Rescues from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Great Mercy Who Removes Transgressions.

Today, the master of repentance in this Daoist ritual, together with the great assembly, reverently beseech the Supreme Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy below, all the Venerable Ones and Sages, all the Great Heavenly Immortals, all the Great Earthly Immortals, the Immortal Hosts of the Five Sacred Peaks, all the Great Perfected Lords, all the Great Perfected Ones, and all the Divine Youths—pervading the ten directions, filling the realms of profound emptiness, and manifesting under every name as all the true and sacred beings. May they together bestow their responsive grace to rescue and protect all beings. May the master of repentance, so-and-so, who undertakes this matter, obtain a response in accordance with their heart, all through the power of this repentance.

May the afflicted recover from illness, may calamities be averted, may those who have passed afar be reborn, may those who have recently departed attain liberation, may the living receive benefit, and may all their prayers be fulfilled. Furthermore, may the four kinds of birth and the six paths of existence all receive this grace; may the spirits of plants and trees, and the lingering souls of the forsaken, seize this auspicious opportunity to ascend together to the Great Dao.

One bow.

**Chapter Two: Repaying Kindness and Offering Merit**

Today, in this Daoist ritual, each member of the great assembly directs their heart and mind, reverently beseeching the Merciful Venerable One to universally bestow boundless merit and virtue upon all people. Now, the causes and effects of repaying kindness are expounded.

The master of repentance, so-and-so, humbly reflects and listens attentively to the scriptural words: When a person is born, Heaven and Earth serve as their model; they bear the yin and embrace the yang, receiving shelter within the womb, their life suspended by Heaven. The Heavenly Emperor then summons the Youth Who Records Lifespans to traverse the human realm, examining and measuring sins and blessings, the fortune or misfortune of men and women, the brevity or length of their lives. Every three days, a report is made; every seven days, a memorial is submitted; every hundred days, a record is finalized—unceasing even for a moment.

If one cultivates goodness and establishes merit, the Divine Youths of the Heavens, the Lords of Life and the Recorders of Deeds, will extend their years and eliminate calamities. If one commits sins and accumulates evil, the Heavenly Kings and the demonic spirits of the Six Heavens will seize their hun and po souls, bringing them before the Three Officials to have their consciousnesses collected. If one’s allotted lifespan is not fulfilled, it is due to the sins they have committed; if one completes their allotted lifespan, it is due to the goodness they have accumulated.

When a person seeks to extend their lifespan, it falls under the jurisdiction of the Earthly Offices. The various Heavens and Emperors examine and verify according to the registers, determining life and death. They then dispatch the officials of the Three Realms and the Youth Who Observes Life to gather the spirit and soul, cutting off the breath of life. If a person is afflicted by prolonged illness, bedridden and gravely stricken, their life nearing its end, and if their family and kin, according to their means, establish a Daoist ritual, recite scriptures, and perform repentance—regardless of the number of scrolls—the family and kin may reverently face the various Heavens and Sages, confessing the karmic offenses of the sick person’s embodied existence, thereby releasing their spirit and soul, extending their lifespan, and restoring them to health.

If the great limit of life is imminent, one may still be rescued through the performance of extensive merit and virtue, dedicating it to the departed soul to spare them from suffering and distress. The living will face no hardship or terror. From the first seventh-day period after death to the three annual commemorations, during the days of ancestral remembrance, offerings of incense and lamps should be made tirelessly, day and night.

Why is this so? There are also the Youths Who Observe Life who monitor and report sins and blessings. If one enters the gate of life, blessings flow to their descendants, they do not linger in hell, and they suffer no karmic retribution. It is like a person initially entangled in a legal dispute, where the case remains unresolved—this is analogous to the situation of the newly deceased.

Thus, two spirits, one of good and one of evil, descend every ten days to inspect the household. For those who perform merit, the good spirit will advocate for them, enabling rebirth in Heaven. For those who do not perform merit, the evil spirit will record their deeds, leading them into confinement, causing their family to experience much fear and misfortune. If there is suffering, one may go to a Daoist abbey or remain at home, facing the image of the Venerable One, bowing to the manifest and hidden transformations, performing purification rituals and practicing the Dao, redeeming karmic offenses to attain liberation. Their names will be inscribed in the registers of immortals, and their bodies will dwell in carefree joy.

Such are the various causes and effects of repaying kindness and offering merit, which are foremost and truly worthy of praise. If there are good men and good women who, for the sake of their parents and all their kin, paint or sculpt images, construct halls, and vow with sincere faith to widely encourage and exhort others—such actions are inconceivable. All people, within the various dharmas, who arouse a single good thought or make a single vow, harboring a heart of gratitude and repayment, are called good fruits, and are inconceivable.

Today, the great assembly in this Daoist ritual, as spoken in the scriptures, reverently beseech the Merciful Venerable One to expound this Dharma gate of merit and virtue for all sentient beings, serving as a path through life and death—this is inconceivable. The master of repentance, so-and-so, for the sake of their nine generations of ancestors, seven generations of forebears, parents, uncles, brothers, themselves, and all their kin—whether in hell, as hungry ghosts, as animals, or among all beings with consciousness—who have not yet received offerings or performed repayment, now wholeheartedly bows in reverence to the true and sacred beings invoked by name. May this merit and virtue pervade both the living and the deceased, enabling all to attain liberation.

Today, humbly for the sake of peace and the offering of merit through this repentance text, prostrating with the five limbs touching the ground, the heart directs its thoughts. Bowing to the Merciful Venerable One, I reverently bow to the true and sacred beings.

With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Clarity Who Bestows Blessings.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Rescues from Suffering at the Sound of Cries.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the True Sovereign and Mysterious Spirit.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Pervades and Observes the Dharma Realm.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Wondrous Light and Profound Stillness.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Nine-Colored Majestic Radiance.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Expedient Means for Liberation.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Receives Blessings in Every Direction.

With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Guards the Soul Without Hindrance.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Turns the Dharma in Accordance with the Heart.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of True Emptiness.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great Perfected.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Transports and Delivers.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Majestic Spirit.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the True Rank.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Profound Subtlety.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Jeweled Mystery.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Void Sovereign.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Compassionate Response and Primordial Harmony.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Compassionate Virtue Who Rescues from Tribulation.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Vastly Saves in the Cinnabar Landscape.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Preserves Life and Protects Destiny.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Supreme Unity Who Rescues from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Universal Compassion Who Protects the Realm.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Carefree Joy.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Grants Rebirth According to Wishes.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Expanse.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of the Ocean of Merit and Virtue.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Dharma Liberation.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Jeweled Radiance.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Great Compassion Who Rescues from Suffering.
With sincere devotion, I bow to the Perfected of Great Mercy Who Eradicates Transgressions.

Today, the master of repentance in this Daoist ritual, along with the great assembly, take refuge in the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the Lower Realm, all the Venerable Ones and Sages, all the Great Perfected, all the Perfected of Wondrous Conduct, all the Great Divine Youths, who pervade the ten directions, fill the boundless void, and manifest throughout all realms. May they, by the power of great compassion, the power of great mercy, the power of the Dao, and the power of the Dharma, universally illuminate the worlds below, the Nine Dark Prisons of Fengdu. May the master of repentance, [Name], their nine generations of ancestors, seven generations of descendants, teachers, parents, uncles, brothers, themselves, and all their kin—whether dwelling in the Three Evil Paths, yet to attain liberation, whether departed long ago or recently passed—all ascend today through sincere repentance. Regardless of the weight of their transgressions, may they together attain liberation and take refuge in the Great Dao.

One bow.

**Chapter Three: The Circulation of Teachings**

Today, the great assembly in this Daoist ritual, each with focused mind, take refuge and repent, gazing reverently upon the Compassionate Venerable One, to expound the teachings of salvation and the circulation of all dharmas.

The master of repentance, [Name], collects their thoughts and listens attentively as the scriptures are revealed: The Primordial Beginning, with one qi, transformed into three qi, dividing into the Three Heavens. The realms of the Three Clarities emerged from the Three Caverns’ treasure scriptures. Thus, the Three Vehicles conjoined the soaring mystery of qi, naturally forming chapters—jade characters and golden writings, dragon scripts and phoenix seals—each a great square of one zhang, with eight corners radiating light. They taught the heavens and circulated through the worlds, turning the Dharma Wheel for five kalpas from beginning to end.

Though heaven and earth may end their course, the Three Caverns shall never perish. They open the path for all beings, guiding humans and gods across the Three Realms and ten directions, all receiving benefit.

It is asked: When did the Three Caverns descend to the world? Did they come simultaneously, or in succession?

The Compassionate Venerable One replied: At the beginning of each kalpa, the Cavern of Perfection descends to transform the world. People embraced virtue and power, dwelling in emptiness and non-being. All upheld the true and correct, attaining long life without death. Next, the Cavern of Mystery descended. The great simplicity had already declined, the pure wind had scattered, and people gradually became frivolous, losing the Dao and rebelling against virtue. Then, the Cavern of Spirit descended. People grew even more frivolous, failing to uphold the great teachings, turning from truth toward falsehood, their lifespans shortening. When the Three Caverns ceased to function, worldly wisdom flourished daily. Humans and ghosts intermingled, the kalpa’s end drew near, lifespans fell below a hundred years, impermanence prevailed in every thought, and ruin never ceased.

I have descended again to proclaim the Three Caverns, spreading transformation among humanity, adapting to the capacities of each era, and propagating the scriptural teachings. Moreover, the Sacred Ancestors have manifested in the human realm to save and deliver sentient beings, expounding precepts and regulations. Whether among the Yi or Xia, whether sages or commoners, they pervaded the ten directions, universally enabling liberation. The wondrous Dharma of the Three Caverns, scattered throughout the world, exhorts sentient beings to diligently cultivate and practice.

Those who accumulate transgressions and karmic burdens, sinking into evil paths, unable to believe and uphold the teachings, follow only falsehoods and various deceptive spirits. They exhaust body and mind, only to descend into hell. Those who believe in and uphold the great Dharma of the Three Caverns shall all enter the Hall of Blessings. Some ascend in broad daylight, others escape through corpse liberation, their forms vanishing into hidden realms. Though their names and traces remain, they secretly traverse the unseen worlds, unknown to others.

Furthermore, it is said: After I withdraw, demonic teachings will flourish. People will die young, wars, floods, and fires will follow one after another, diseases will linger, and suffering will persist day and night. Wealth and treasures will be exhausted in service to deceitful spirits, falsehoods will multiply daily, and the frivolous and deceitful will spread with the times. Hunger, cold, and misery will drive fathers and sons to wander, never awakening.

Again, I reflect upon you all, sunk in the depths of kalpas: I speak these essential words to enlighten the deaf and blind.

Moreover, the scriptures teach sentient beings to recognize the root and origin, the causes of past lives, the retribution of sin and blessing, the auspicious and inauspicious, the gates of life and death, and the means of expedient practice. They urge turning from evil to embrace goodness, preserving life and nature, attaining long life and non-action, and taking refuge in the Great Dao. Those who preserve them shall receive blessings; those who cultivate them shall be divinely protected.

Thus, the Perfected of Wondrous Conduct, divine beings, and immortals of the heavens always desire that people diligently burn incense and repent, so that benevolent spirits will protect them and the multitude of sages will bestow their thoughts. If one bears transgressions, bound internally and externally, malevolent spirits will wreak havoc, diseases will afflict, and disasters—water, fire, blades, poisonous creatures, fierce beasts, shackles, and prisons—will bring inescapable suffering.

If one only adorns the exterior—face, clothing, hands, and feet—yet fails to inwardly cleanse the body, mind, roots of transgression, and evil karma, are they not foolish and deluded? Just as the face, hands, feet, and clothing, when diligently washed and scrubbed, must become pure.

The Supreme Pole Perfected One spoke: When the Heavenly Worthy was in the Fragrant Accumulation World of the Heaven of Blessed Virtue, expounding the Dao amidst the assembly of celestial immortals, he thought of the Universally Beneficent Perfected One, who arose with fearless power and extended his mind of vast compassion. For the sake of all sentient beings, he inquired about karmic conditions and proclaimed the responsive titles of the various Honored Ones.

At that moment, the earth turned to the hue of refined gold, and the heavens rained down precious flowers, fragrant incense, and wondrous treasures, all drifting through the void to fill the space before the Dao, beyond count. "All you sentient beings, you ought to believe and uphold this, exert yourselves with sincere devotion, propagate my teachings, and not allow external demons to disrupt and disturb the realm."

When the Universally Beneficent Perfected One and the assembly of celestial beings heard these words, they wept in longing and admiration, choked with sorrow, as if they had lost their parents. They vowed that the Merciful Honored One would constantly admonish and instruct them, so that they might awaken and realize the supreme Dao.

Thereupon, the Universally Beneficent addressed the assembly of celestial immortals and sages: "In the cities, towns, villages, and tranquil mountain forests of the lands in the ten directions, if there are diligent scholar-immortals, or pure and faithful officials and clansmen who protect and uphold the scriptures and repentances, reverently invoking the responsive titles of the transformation bodies—if they delight in paper and ink, copying and binding the scrolls with silk cords, adorning them with the seven treasures, and exhorting the people of the realm to bow in worship and make offerings as if facing the true form, unwavering day and night, circulating and proclaiming them so that those who have not heard may hear and those who have not seen may see—those who cultivate in accordance with the Dao shall be protected by the assemblies of celestial immortals, jade maidens, and the ten divisions of mighty spirits. Such persons shall forever attain peace and happiness, fulfill their aspirations, and this majestic power is inconceivable, like the boundless void, impossible to exhaust."

Today, in this Daoist ritual assembly, as the scriptures declare, the responsive titles of the various Honored Ones are inconceivable. May all sentient beings—those who have already suffered or have yet to suffer—all attain liberation. The repentance master [Name] today prostrates for peace and offers this repentance text, bowing with the five limbs to the ground, wholeheartedly invoking: "We bow our heads to the Merciful Honored One, reverently paying homage to the true sages."

With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Jade Clarity who bestows blessings.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who rescues from suffering at the sound of cries.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Divine Grotto.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who harmonizes spirits and benefits beings.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who embodies the myriad virtues.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of boundless illumination.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of perfect fulfillment in the myriad practices.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of primordial yang’s transformative measure.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who expounds the Dao and pervades transformation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the six penetrations who relieves suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of true intention.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Purple Palace.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who roams and abides.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Lotus Flower.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of silent contemplation.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the lofty perfected.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Mysterious Palace.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of unimpeded freedom.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of universal moisture and non-action.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who universally ferries across like a boat and oar.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of supreme virtue and luminous countenance.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the Great One who rescues from suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who bestows longevity and preserves life.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of carefree joy.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy who grants rebirth according to one’s wishes.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of universal compassion who protects the realm.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of boundless expanse.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of the ocean of merit and virtue.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Universally Beneficent Perfected One.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Universally Saving Perfected One.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Greatly Compassionate Perfected One who rescues from suffering.
With sincere devotion, we pay homage to the Greatly Merciful Perfected One who extracts transgressions.

Today, the repentance master of this ritual assembly and the great assembly, gazing upward, vow that the Most High Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy of the lower realm, the various Honored Ones and sages, the lofty immortals of the Golden Towers, the sagely emperors of the Jade Capital, the dragon spirits and earth gods, the true officials of villages and domains, the celestial immortals and lords of the grotto-heavens, the assemblies of immortals throughout the ten directions, the entire expanse of the mysterious void, and all the manifested true sages—by their inconceivable power and boundless merit and virtue—may enable the repentance master [Name], prostrating for peace and offering this repentance text, to uplift the nine generations of ancestors and the seven lineages, the recently departed and the long-deceased, parents and the six relations, and all kin. Through this repentance, may they transcend to the Land of Ultimate Bliss, not linger in the three evil destinies, nor tread the five sufferings. May all living kin, close and distant relatives, and all branches of the family tree attain lasting peace and be forever free from suffering.

Moreover, may those who seek to avert misfortune, those who seek to repay karmic debts, those burdened by karma, and those afflicted by illness—all, by the power of this repentance, forever rely on the great Dao.

One bow.

Chapter Four: Manifest Verification and True Realization

Today, in this ritual assembly, each person directs their mind, bows in homage, and takes refuge, gazing up to the Merciful Honored One, manifesting the repentance dharma and verifying the karmic conditions. The repentance master [Name], gathering their mind and kneeling reverently, listens attentively to the scriptural words: "The Dao gives rise to the one qi, which divides and transforms into the three powers. Responding to the world, it establishes names and manifests titles according to conditions, pervading the dharma-realm, as numerous as the grains of dust. Furthermore, there are accomplished scholar-immortals who have ascended to the highest ranks among the heavens, also beyond count.

If there are good men and good women who can arouse the natural intention of the Dao, serving as rulers, kings, queens, consorts, dukes, and the people of the realm, as well as the nine generations of ancestors, the seven lineages, teachers, parents, themselves, and all kin—even those in the three evil destinies, the five sufferings, the eight difficulties, and the nine dark realms—who day and night practice the Dao, burn incense, scatter flowers, light lamps, and bow in worship to the titles of the Heavenly Worthies, then the Heavenly Worthies of the ten directions and their countless assemblies will together come to witness and record their merits among the heavens. Their own blessings and longevity shall be boundless, disasters will vanish, transgressions will be extinguished, the realm will be at peace, the people will be at ease, the three evil destinies will cease their opposition, the five sufferings will halt their bitterness, and all stagnant sentient beings will attain liberation."

At that time, the Perfected One of the Great Ultimate addressed the Master of Mystic Words, saying: "Always with this scripture and the transformative titles of the Heavenly Worthy, circulate and widely disseminate them, that they may pervade the ten directions. Let all men and women copy, enshrine, and reverently recite them, and they shall invoke the Ten Flower Perfected Ones, the Vajra Warriors, the Five Emperors of the Three Realms, and all majestic spirits to guard their lands and protect their people. If one establishes images wherever one dwells, the merit shall be immeasurable.

If there be male or female officials of the Dharma-body who, on the ten straight days of the first and last of the month, the Three Origins, the Eight Festivals, the days of their own life-destiny and the Geng-Shen, and the assemblies of the twelfth month, wish for the peace of the realm, quiet their minds, and silently recite the titles of the Heavenly Worthy, then they shall be met by immortals descending to receive them, and cloud-cranes coming to welcome them.

If one extols and praises, exhorting all men and women to receive, uphold, and recite these sacred images, the merit is truly inconceivable.

If there be sentient beings who, upon seeing the compassionate titles of the Heavenly Worthy, harbor disbelief, slight the Dharma-treasure, and doubt or slander the sacred texts, know that such persons have, from kalpas without measure, sunk into the lower ghosts, enduring manifold sufferings and passing through strange forms, only now to be reborn into the human realm. Foolish and blind, they comprehend nothing, habituated to evil causes, unable to believe or revere.

If there be sentient beings who, upon hearing this repentance ritual—be it a single sentence, a single verse, a single title, a single bow—generate a mind of faith, know that such persons in former lives once entered the jeweled city, heard the wondrous Dharma, and entered the jeweled treasury, where they personally read and recited. Now reborn, their faith and devotion only deepen.

If one initially holds this repentance ritual in reverence but later regrets, ceasing to bow or recite, and allows the mind to grow indolent, know that such a person, though possessing a human body, has not yet severed their strange forms. After this life’s transgressions, they shall again fall into evil destinies, suffering for ten thousand kalpas without hope of liberation."

At that time, the Perfected One of the Great Ultimate completed the transmission of the scripture, and the Master of Mystic Words bowed his head in reverence and thanks. Then, moved by the true words, he received the seven transformative titles of the Heavenly Worthy, to be imparted to sentient beings for the salvation of the living and the deliverance of the dead. Thus, all beings shall be shown how to recite them without neglecting the sacred teachings.

Today, in this ritual arena, the repentance-master [Name], prostrating for [specific matter], bows in worship to this repentance text. With five limbs touching the earth and a single mind, he raises his thought, bows his head to the Compassionate Worthy, and reverently salutes the true sages:

With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Transformative Titles.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Pervades All Actions.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Boundless Wisdom.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Constant Non-Action.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Fills Empty Space.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy of Constant Purity.
With a sincere mind, I bow to the Heavenly Worthy Who Responds to Conditions.

Today, the repentance-master of this ritual arena and the great assembly, looking up, vow that the Seven Transformative Titles of the Heavenly Worthy of the Supreme Numinous Treasure from the ten directions shall together lend their virtuous power to shelter and protect all beings. May the repentance-master [Name] fulfill his heart’s wishes, and may all karmic retributions and opposing forces be dissolved. May all living kin be free from obstacles and calamities, their misfortunes severed. Further, may they gain keen intelligence and profound virtue, their merits complete and their conduct perfected, their official and scholarly aspirations fulfilled, their achievements towering, their honors ever-renewed. May inner and outer realms alike know well-being, with superiors and inferiors in proper order. May weapons be stilled, winds and rains timely, and longevity prolonged. May their names be inscribed on jade tablets, one act of merit repaid ten thousandfold, eternally without end. Life after life, may they forever escape sinking and drowning. May their descendants continue for a hundred million years."

May all sentient beings together ascend the Dao’s shore.

**First Bow**
The Immortal Lord Ge Xuan proclaimed: The Most High Lord Lao said, "All the Heavenly Worthies of the Ten Directions are born of the Primordial Beginning in response to qi, abiding and pacifying the lands, teaching and guiding sentient beings. According to karmic conditions and perceptions, they scatter their reflections and divide their bodies, transforming endlessly. With the turning of kalpas, they appear and vanish without constancy, opening the path to salvation for all, their blessings extending across the ten thousand heavens.

If Daoist priests, female officials, and all men and women can arouse a heart of goodness—for the sake of the ruler, parents, wives and children, themselves and their kin, the

May all be freed from suffering and universally attain liberation.
May all awaken to non-action and together ascend the Dao’s fruit.

**First Bow**
Here ends the Tenth Scroll of *The Most High’s Compassionate Dao-Field: The Nine Dark Realms Repentance Rite for Dispelling Disasters*.
